//====================================================
// File 091
//====================================================

// NOTE:
// this whole event, and the next two, are not used.
// i spent several hours taking apart the game's event
// trigger system just to make sure of this
// (because boy did i not want to have to redo the
// robot select screen beyond what i've already done).
// these events are not flagged to be able to occur
// after any mission, and their queue functions aren't
// manually triggered either.
// basically, it looks like they originally planned to
// allow you to use asmodeus in the main story, not
// just battle mode, but ended up deciding against it.
// this would have become possible to trigger at some
// point in the story as long as you had at least
// 99,999 million yen.

#STARTFILE(091)

//====================================================
// File 103
//====================================================

// this appears to be unused.
// my best guess is that it was used to develop/test
// a mission during development, and never got deleted.
// it seems to be an amalgam of two of the earlier
// tutorials, suggesting they were originally one
// long mission that got split up later.
// but who knows?

#STARTFILE(103)

//[TEXT]
#STARTSTRING(0x65AC, 0xB2, 0x65AA, 0x0)
// the game has this in a section labeled "MISSION_EX",
// which would normally be the mission explanation.
// but in this case, it's programmed to display a few
// dialogue boxes of gibberish.
// without modifying the script, the game then
// immediately goes to the damage report and ends the
// mission.
// modifying it to skip this part reveals that it consists
// of a primitive scene with no voice acting or
// text box portraits, which then cuts to an early
// version of the "now loading" screen over which
// most of the remaining text plays.
// the game then freezes immediately after closing
// the box.
// whether there's any actual mission logic in there,
// i don't know.

// \@02折刀暇寂辞売縁借族貧乏誉母嬉崖換側悟円賠償視貨橋倉南弁概末鋭\n
// 駆払隔魅劣斬蹴浮熱線彩推鋼轟靴

\w

// \n
// 空個榴検和散貯金祈手闊弾刃裂章池健兆

\w
\c

// 手榴弾闊歩猛遭\@00脅威綺麗

\w

// 港湾施設

\w


#ENDSTRING()

The Jet Robot {Vordan} will deploy momentarily.
